 We are very happy
 I've lived with depression on and off since i was about 13 years old
 This is not a revelation or a confession
 Those who know me know this about me
 It's not something i take any pains to hide, I'm not ashamed of it or particularly troubled by it
 It's just a part of who i am
 i have days where i feel good and then i have days where i don't
 One minute everything's fine and the next it's like someone turned the light off inside my head
 i go quiet and it's difficult to get out of bed
 Like it always does the world around me loses focus and i struggle to make sense of it
 Sometimes these bouts last an hour - sometimes they last days
 Today, I'm on day 4
 i say i live with depression rather than i struggle with it because for me (and i speak only for myself here) i don't see why it has to be a struggle
 i once read an idea by an American essayist called Richard Mitchell which stayed with me; it's now become how i try to approach the dips in my week or month
 The idea is this: To be sick, or to suffer, is inevitable
 But to become bitter and vindictive in sickness and suffering and to surrender to irrationality, supposing yourself the innocent and virtuous victim of the evils intentions of the world, is not inevitable
 The appropriate answer to the question - Why me? is the other question - Why not me? *** Why am i writing about this? Well, i spend a fair amount of time on social media during the course of my day and today i found myself looking for something to post because it's been a few days since I've posted anything
 i couldn't find anything so i figured I'd just talk about this - how I'm doing, instead of what I'm doing
 It's as simple as that, and we could all stand to do a little more of it

 An average of 18 officers in the country's most influential Indian Administrative Service (IAS) are taking voluntary retirement every year
 pichley 10 saalon ke dauraan 181 iees adhikariyon ne svaichhik sevanivritti lee he
 This information has been received under Right to Information (RTI)
 ek iees adhikari ke prashikshan main sarkaar ke chaar lakh rupee kharch hote hai, lekin kuch iees adhikari bahurashtriya evam kansaltency companiyon main adhik vetan or ucch pad kii chahat main svaichhik sevanivritti le rahe hai
 Many of such executives who take voluntary retirement get involved with large companies
 kuch samay pehle iees adhikari eke khurana ke svaichhik sevanivritti lene ke baad jepieske sports se, jepi aryaa ke jepi ganga infrastracchar limited, em sambashiwa raav ke heritage food limited, vivek kulkarni ke bi2ke corporation, pisi sirus ke jivan telecom, bies patil ke suprajith ejineering limited, ke nilakshan ke kansaltency form se judane kii khabar ai thi
 On this subject, former CBI Director RK Raghavan says that the officers of the Indian Administrative Service today are not at liberty to take automatic decisions on any subject and they are forced to work under various political pressures
 yah ieses adhikariyon ke svaichhik sevanivritti lene kaa sabase pramukh kaaran he
 Apart from this, the desire to work in high salaries and top positions in the private sector is also a reason for this

 darasal, ye vyakhyaayein ekangi hai or suvidhanusaar chaynit hai

 aise main, sangh pramukh kaa itane bade or prachaarit manch se kam se kam baar-baar vividhta yaa bahulata kii baat karnaa, pranab babu ke nagpur daure kii ek ahm khabar thi
 a major part of Pranab Mukherjee's speech was immersed in the syrup of Hinduism

 yaad rakhanevaali baat ye he ki pranab mukherjee bengal ke jis raajnneetik prishthbhumi se aate hai vah vam-varchasv kaa daur he jise kai log ‚Äòvam-aatank‚Äô kaa bhi daur kehete hai

 aadhe ghante ke bhaashan main mukherjee sari baaten kah bhi nahin sakate the, aise manchon par ishaaron main kaaphi baaten kahi jaati he
 Pranab Babu unequivocally acknowledged that Ghori's invasion was a Muslim invader invasion in the 12th century and that Muslims ruled India for nearly 600 years (contrary to the general propaganda that India had a Muslim rule for a thousand years!) He spent much time on Hindu history, even after the recent events and clear facts were available, he consolidated the history of Muslim rule into a single force

 yah mulat: europea rashtrawaad kii avadharana kii carbon copy he

 sangh pramukh ke bhaashan main kuch acchhee baaten thim to kuch ascharyajanak bhi thi

 mohan bhagwat ne kaha ki hamaara desh sujal, sufal, malayaj or ‚Äòprakritik rup se surakshit mathrubhumi he‚Äô jahaan ‚Äòbahari logon kaa aana janaa kam ho saktaa tha‚Äô!yah itihasbodh apane mul main galat he

 purv kendriya mantri shakeel ahamed ko birender singh kii jagah dilli kaa prabharee banaaya gaya he
 Birender Singh has been removed from the post of general secretary
 dilli, madhya pradesh, chhattisgarh or rajasthan main isi varsh vidhansabha ke chunaav karaae jaaenge
 Ahmed has also been given the charge of Haryana, Punjab and Union Territory of Chandigarh

 mahasachiv ke rup main kaamat rajasthan, gujarat, dadar evam nagar haveli or daman evam div ke prabharee banaae gaye hai

 shanivaar ko hi kendriya mantrimandal se istipha dene vaale seepi joshi ko assam, bihar, pashchim bengal or andaman evam nicobar dweep samooh kaa prabharee banaaya gaya he
 Jardan Dwivedi will be in charge of All India Congress Committee (AICC) meetings, AICC departments, CWC, organizations, organizational elections, sessions and coordination
 mukul vaasanic ko mahasachiv ke rup main kerala, puddcheri, tamilnadu or lakshadweep kaa prabharee banaaya gaya he, jabaki luijinho falerio arunachal pradesh, manipur, meghalaya, mizoram, nagaland, sikkim or tripura ke prabharee honge

 gulchain singh charak, jagadish titalar or jagamit singh baraar ko bhi hataaya gaya he

 pherbadal main kuch party mahasachivon or sachivon ko hataa diya gaya he

 guuruuvaar ko adaalat ne rawalpindi sthit adiyaala jail main sunwaayee ke dauraan yah bhi nirdesh diya ki ajmal kasaab or anya dwaara istemaal kii gai naavon ko bharat se waapas laayaa janaa chahie or use maamle se judi vastu banaaya jaae
 a court official said that the trial court has directed the Director General of Federal Investigation Agency to produce all the 24 Indian witnesses in the court so that their statements can be recorded
 iske alaava adaalat ne yah bhi nirdesh diya ki ajmal kasaab dwaara istemaal kii gai naav ko pakistan laayaa jaae, kyonki yah maamle se sambandhit vastu he or isaki puri jaanch honi chahie
 The official said that the Ministry of Home Affairs will write a letter to the Ministry of External Affairs in this regard
 unhone kaha ki pakistani ayog ne 2012 main jin chaar pramukh bhartiya gavaahon ke bayaan darj kiye the, ve nichali adaalat main sweekaar nahin kyonki bharat sarkaar ne unase jirah kii anumati nahin di thi
 The eight-member judicial commission had recorded the statement of senior inspector Ramesh Mahale, who investigated the Mumbai attack
 ayog ne apni kaarywahi samaapt karne se pehle do chikitsakon ke bayaan bhi darj kiye the, jinhone mumbai hamale main maare gaye logon tathaa suraksha balon dwaara maar giraaye gaye aatankwaadiyon kaa postmortem kiya tha
 Magistrate RV Sawant Waghule had recorded Kasab's confession and immediately recorded Kasab's statement after his arrest
 nyaayik ayog ne pakistani kii aatankwaad nirodhak adaalat kii taraf se bharat kaa daura kiya tha
 It was believed that the statements of Indian witnesses would be used as evidence in the lower court
 yadhyapi lakhvi ke vakil ne ayog kii kaarywahi ko chunauti di kyonki mukhya metropalitan magistrate es es scindia ne uske sadasyon ko gavaahon se jirah kii ijaajat nahin di
 The lower court here declared the commission's proceedings illegal
 pakistani adhikariyon ne hamale kii yojana main shaamil lashkare taiyaba ke saat sadasyon ko giraftaar kiya he
 The comments lakhvi ke alaava anya giraftaar lashkare taiyaba ke sadasyon main abdul waajid, mazhar ikbaal, sadik, shahid jameel, jameel ahamed or younus anjum shaamil hai
 All these have been going on trial in the anti-terrorism Court since 2009

 Filmmaker Karan Johar broke his silence on Tuesday by releasing an emotional video on the controversy surrounding his film 'ae Dil Hai Mushkil'
 johar ne pakkaa bharosa dilaate hue kaha ki vah bhavishya main 'padosi desh kii pratibhaaon ko mauka nahin denge', lekin iske saath hi unhone jald relies hone vaali apni film 'i dil he mushkil' kii vakaalat karte hue usko target nahin karne kii apil bhi kii
 Protesting the demand for a section to be banned from the film 'ae Dil Hai Mushkil', which also stars Pakistani actors, Johar said, '
 
 
 main aapse vinati karata hum ki is cheez par dhyaan den
 
 
 That is, more than 300 Indians in my crew have shed their blood and sweat in this film
 
 
 aise main main nahin samajhataa ki anya bharatiyon kii ore se kiya jane vaala yah virodh unke liye nyaaysangat hoga
 (film director Anurag Kashyap said, so i thought it more appropriate to 'talk directly to PM Modi') 44 saal ke nirmaataa ne kaha ki vah itane dinon tak isliye chup the, kyonki vah is baat se 'vyathit or gahari pidaa main the' ki log unhen rashtravirohi samaj rahe the
 Karan insisted, 'when i shot my film in september-december last year, the atmosphere and circumstances were completely different

 Because i feel the same way
 ' It is to be noted that a group of about 450 cinema owners has said that they did not perform those films after keeping in mind the public sentiments after the terror attack in Uri, Kashmir (in which 19 soldiers were martyred) last month
 Which are Pakistani artists
 yah association single screen cinemaaon se kaaphi had tak judaa he, lekin multiplex se nahin

 the

 mangalvaar subah hi film ke nirmaataaon ne mumbai police se 28 oktober ko relies hone ja rahi 'i dil he mushkil' ko pradarshit karne ja rahe cinemagharon ko suraksha pradaan karne kii apil kii he
 The comments paak ke kabje vaale kashmir main bhartiya sena kii sargical strike ke baad tanaav main badhotaree ke baad mumbai main nirmaataaon kii ek body ne haal hi main pakistani kalakaaron ke bhartiya filmon main kaam karne ko lekar bain laga diya he
 In retaliation, Pakistani theater owners have also decided to stop screening of Indian films
